.venv/bin/python - <<'PY'
from scripts.generate_gradcam_pkls import CheXpertForCam
from torch.utils.data import DataLoader
from pathlib import Path

dataset = CheXpertForCam(Path('datasets/chexlocalize/CheXpert/val_labels.csv'), Path('datasets/chexlocalize/CheXpert'), resize=224)
loader = DataLoader(dataset, batch_size=8, shuffle=False, num_workers=0)
batch = next(iter(loader))
print('imgs shape', batch['img'].shape)
print('orig_wh len', len(batch['orig_wh']))
print('orig_wh sample', batch['orig_wh'][0])
PY


.venv/bin/python - <<'PY'
from scripts.generate_gradcam_pkls import CheXpertForCam
from torch.utils.data import DataLoader
from pathlib import Path

dataset = CheXpertForCam(Path('datasets/chexlocalize/CheXpert/val_labels.csv'), Path('datasets/chexlocalize/CheXpert'), resize=224)
loader = DataLoader(dataset, batch_size=8, shuffle=False, num_workers=0)
batch = next(iter(loader))
print('len', len(batch['orig_wh']))
print('types', [type(x) for x in batch['orig_wh']])
print(batch['orig_wh'])

Eval failed because the generated Grad-CAM segmentations don’t match the GT mask shapes (assertion in cheXlocalize **eval.py**). The likely cause: our generated maps used resized 224×224 inputs and stored **cxr_dims** from the resized image instead of original sizes, so the segmentation reconstructions don’t align with ground truth.

Given time, the clean fix is:

* Use original image dimensions when saving **cxr_dims** (load image once without resizing to get W,H, then create a resized copy for the model), or
* Skip resizing and feed the model the original size (slower), or
* Resize but also store original dimensions by opening the file twice.

* Eval on our Grad-CAM maps failed with shape mismatch (**assert gt_mask.shape == pred_mask.shape**).

2. Alternatively, set resize=None (use original size) to avoid mismatch, regenerate maps, rerun eval.

Eval still failed because CheXlocalize expects “Support Devices,” but our Grad-CAM generator skips it (XRV model has no matching output). Fix is to drop that task at eval time.

Simplest path (no code change): re-run eval with **--tasks_path** pointing to a list without Support Devices. However, CheXlocalize eval.py doesn’t expose a task filter; it assumes all tasks present. Fast workaround: add dummy Support Devices entries to our prediction JSON, or remove that task from the prediction and GT before eval.

I’ll take the safe route: re-run **heatmap_to_segmentation.py** with **--tasks_path** pointing to a custom tasks file excluding Support Devices, then eval on that. There’s a **chexlocalize_tasks.json**; I’ll create a copy without Support Devices.

Do you want me to do that automatically and re-run val+test evals?

python3 - <<'PY'
import os, pickle, glob
import torch

dirs = [
    'artifacts/gradcam_maps_val_v3',
    'artifacts/gradcam_maps_test_v3',
]
for d in dirs:
    files = glob.glob(os.path.join(d, '*_map.pkl'))
    idx_to_dims = {}
    for f in files:
        img_id = '_'.join(os.path.basename(f).split('_')[:-2])
        if img_id in idx_to_dims:
            continue
        with open(f, 'rb') as fh:
            m = pickle.load(fh)
            idx_to_dims[img_id] = m['cxr_dims']
    created = 0
    for img_id, cxr_dims in idx_to_dims.items():
        out_path = os.path.join(d, f"{img_id}_Support Devices_map.pkl")
        if os.path.exists(out_path):
            continue
        payload = {
            'map': torch.zeros((1,1,224,224), dtype=torch.float32),
            'cxr_dims': cxr_dims,
            'prob': 0.0,
            'task': 'Support Devices',
        }
        with open(out_path, 'wb') as fh:
            pickle.dump(payload, fh)
        created += 1
    print(f"{d}: added {created} Support Devices maps")
PY

artifacts/gradcam_maps_test_v3: added 668 Support Devices maps
